[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark IRC [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol dissector during fuzzing tests. The issue occurs in the [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_irc_names` function when processing IRC NAMES commands, resulting in a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite operation that exceeds the allocated buffer size by [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes. This is a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-byte write heap-buffer-overflow with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m45[0m[39m, indicating a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msignificant security concern.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability, specifically a write operation [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat attempts to write [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes to a memory location immediately after a [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Error Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer detected a WRITE of size [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m at address `[0m[1;36m0x5060001c64f3[0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte heap-allocated region [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m0x5060001c64c0[0m[39m` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x5060001c64f3[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This indicates that the write operation is attempting to write [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwell beyond the boundaries of the allocated buffer.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following call chain:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` which processes a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest case containing IRC protocol data[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Dissection Chain**: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_frame` → `dissect_irc` → `dissect_irc_request` → [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_irc_request_command`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Vulnerable Function**: `dissect_irc_names` at line [0m[1;36m563[0m[39m in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-irc.c[0m[39m`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Operation**: The overflow occurs in `tvb_memcpy` which wraps the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard `memcpy` function[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Details[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic buffer is allocated in `dissect_irc_names` at line [0m[1;36m537[0m[39m using [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`malloc`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocated size is [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m bytes, but the subsequent write operation attempts to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This represents a significant mismatch between allocated size and the amount of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata being copied[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Test Case Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing input that triggers this vulnerability is:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNAMES [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code snippets, I have identified a [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability** in the Wireshark IRC protocol dissector. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue affects three functions that process comma-separated IRC channel names:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **`dissect_irc_names`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m563[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - PRIMARY VULNERABILITY [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreported in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevaluation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **`dissect_irc_join`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m373[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - SAME VULNERABILITY PATTERN[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **`dissect_irc_part`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m438[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m441[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - SAME VULNERABILITY PATTERN[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs when processing comma-separated channel names in a loop:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m548[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m355[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m404[0m[39m**: `length = [0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calculates the TOTAL remaining bytes from `start_offset` to the end [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the buffer[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m549[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m356[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m405[0m[39m**: `end_offset = [0m[1;35mtvb_find_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, start_offset, length, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m','[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` searches for a comma delimiter[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **When a comma IS found** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., `end_offset != [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code should copy only [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`end_offset - start_offset` bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe segment length until the comma[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **VULNERABILITY**: Instead, the code incorrectly uses `length` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotal remaining [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which can be much larger than the allocated buffer size of `CHANNELLEN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m51[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Test Case Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing input demonstrates the bug:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNAMES #[0m[1;35maaaa...[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m125[0m[39m [0m[32m'a'[0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[33m...[0m[39m,#hello\n[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen processing the first channel:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer allocated: [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CHANNELLEN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `length` = [0m[1;36m125[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentire remaining data including [0m[32m",#hello\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Attempted copy: [0m[1;36m132[0m[39m bytes into [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-byte buffer → **OVERFLOW**[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference Implementation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe **`dissect_irc_list`** function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m613[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m616[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the CORRECT [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m613[0m[39m: Correct bounds checking[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m616[0m[39m: Correct segment length[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_list_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend_offset-start_offset, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix `dissect_irc_names` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m525[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m571[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIXED CODE:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, channel_name, start_offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend_offset-start_offset < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**: [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When a comma is found at `end_offset`, we should only copy the bytes from [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`start_offset` to `end_offset` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., `end_offset - start_offset` bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds the channel name limit[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This matches the correct implementation in `dissect_irc_list` at line [0m[1;36m613[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix `dissect_irc_join` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m330[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m379[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m? end_offset-start_offset : CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIXED CODE:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_irc_request_command_join_channel, tvb, start_offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend_offset-start_offset, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same root cause as the other two functions[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both the memory copy and protocol tree item need the segment length fix[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Must match the correct pattern in `dissect_irc_list`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Explanation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: The fix modifies only the incorrect length calculations, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving all other logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern**: All three functions will match the proven-correct [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation in `dissect_irc_list`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Complete Fix**: Addresses both the memory safety issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol tree display issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes**: The functions still parse comma-separated channel [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames correctly, just with proper bounds checking[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory allocation**: No changes to `[0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCHANNELLEN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - still allocates [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same fixed-size buffer[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Loop structure**: No changes to the while loop or comma-finding logic[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Error handling**: No changes to NULL checks or early returns[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Protocol tree structure**: No changes to subtree creation or field types[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Edge cases**: The `end_offset == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno comma found[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m branches already have [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect bounds checking and remain unchanged[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap-buffer-overflow**: By using `end_offset - start_offset` instead of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`length`, we copy only the actual segment length[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Bounds checking**: The ternary operator `[0m[1;39m([0m[39msegment_length < CHANNELLEN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment_length : CHANNELLEN` prevents overflow even if a single segment exceeds [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistency**: All four channel-parsing functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`join`, `part`, `names`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`list`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will have identical bounds checking logic[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Test case**: The fuzzing input with [0m[1;36m125[0m[39m [0m[32m'a'[0m[39ms will now correctly copy only the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment until the comma [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor max [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preventing the overflow[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Long channel names**: If a single channel segment exceeds CHANNELLEN [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m50[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it will be truncated in the `channel_name` buffer[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the intended behavior per IRC RFC [0m[1;36m1459[0m[39m which defines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCHANNELLEN as the maximum[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Note**: The protocol tree display via `proto_tree_add_item` will still show [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe full channel name correctly[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Protocol tree display**: Previously, when a comma was found, the protocol tree[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould incorrectly show all remaining data as a single channel[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Fix**: Now it correctly shows only the segment until the comma[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Users will see the correct channel names in the Wireshark GUI[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backwards compatibility**: No impact on packet capture files or existing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The changes only affect internal buffer management and display[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to network protocol parsing or file formats[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_irc_list` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m613[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m616[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already implements this exact [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern correctly, serving as the reference implementation. This demonstrates that:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fix pattern is already used and proven in the same file[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The same developers likely intended this pattern for all similar functions[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The vulnerability is a copy-paste error or oversight during initial development[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy addresses a critical heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrecting the length calculation when copying comma-separated IRC channel names. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix applies the proven-correct pattern from `dissect_irc_list` to three [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_irc_names`, `dissect_irc_join`, `dissect_irc_part`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring consistent and safe bounds checking across all IRC channel name parsing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
